</p><p>废物（包括石油、有毒液体、污水和垃圾）向海洋的排放是受<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%B3%95" title="国际法">国际法</a>所规管的，《防止倾倒废弃物及其他物质污染海洋的公约》（简称<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1972%E4%BC%A6%E6%95%A6%E5%85%AC%E7%BA%A6" title="1972伦敦公约">1972伦敦公约</a>）是一项为控制废弃物海洋倾倒的<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%9B%BD" title="联合国">联合国</a>协议，截至2012年6月8日已有89个国家批准加入该项公约<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-284"><a href="#cite_note-284">[276]</a></sup>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%98%B2%E6%AD%A2%E8%88%B9%E8%88%B6%E6%B1%A1%E6%9F%93%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E5%85%AC%E7%BA%A6" title="防止船舶污染国际公约">防止船舶污染国际公约</a>（简称MARPOL 73/78）是国际海事组织为控制海上船只对海洋污染行为的国际公约，截至2013年5月已有152个海洋国家批准加入该项公约<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-285"><a href="#cite_note-285">[277]</a></sup>。
</p><p>海洋上大部分的漂浮塑料垃圾并不会进行<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E9%99%8D%E8%A7%A3" title="生物降解">生物降解</a>，即并不会随着时间分解并最终降解到分子水平，一些刚性塑料可以在海上漂浮多年<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-286"><a href="#cite_note-286">[278]</a></sup>。在北太平洋环流中部，有一个永久的<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%AA%E5%B9%B3%E6%B4%8B%E5%9E%83%E5%9C%BE%E5%B8%B6" title="太平洋垃圾带">太平洋垃圾带</a>累积了大量的漂浮塑料废物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-287"><a href="#cite_note-287">[279]</a></sup>，在北大西洋环流中也有个类似的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="North Atlantic garbage patch" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="垃圾带"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9E%83%E5%9C%BE%E5%B8%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="垃圾带（页面不存在）">垃圾带</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Atlantic_garbage_patch" title="en:North Atlantic garbage patch"><span dir="auto" lang="en">North Atlantic garbage patch</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-288"><a href="#cite_note-288">[280]</a></sup>。一些以海洋为觅食带的海鸟，如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E5%A4%A9%E7%BF%81" title="信天翁">信天翁</a>和<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E7%87%95" title="海燕">海燕</a>等，常会误将人类产生的污染漂浮物当作食物并在其消化系统中因不能被消化而积聚，最终导致死亡，一些海龟和鲸鱼的胃中也会常发现有<a href="/wiki/%E5%A1%91%E6%96%99%E8%A2%8B" title="塑料袋">塑料袋</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%B1%BC%E7%BA%BF" title="鱼线">鱼线</a>。而较小的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Microplastics" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="微型塑料"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E5%9E%8B%E5%A1%91%E6%96%99&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="微型塑料（页面不存在）">微型塑料</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microplastics" title="en:Microplastics"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Microplastics</span></a></span>）</span></span>可能会下沉从而危及在海床上的滤食性海洋生物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-289"><a href="#cite_note-289">[281]</a></sup>。
</p><p>海洋中大部分的石油污染是来自于城市和工业制造<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WWF_280-1"><a href="#cite_note-WWF-280">[272]</a></sup>。石油污染对海洋生物的危害巨大，油性物质会使海鸟的羽毛阻塞从而降低羽毛的保暖性和隔水性并减少海鸟的浮力，或当海鸟尝试清理羽毛中的油性物质时会被摄入。虽然<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E6%B4%8B%E5%93%BA%E4%B9%B3%E5%8B%95%E7%89%A9" title="海洋哺乳动物">海洋哺乳动物</a>受石油污染影响的程度没有海鸟所受的程度严重，但是它们也会可能因为清理皮毛上的油性物质而使皮毛的保暖性降低造成体温过低，或被这些石油污染物导致失明、脱水或中毒。而当油性物质下沉时，<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%95%E6%A3%B2%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="底栖生物">底栖无脊椎动物</a>会被淹没，鱼类会中毒，海洋生物链会被破坏。短期来说，石油泄漏会导致海洋生物数量减少和种群失衡、人类的休闲活动会受影响、依赖海洋的人的生计被破坏<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-290"><a href="#cite_note-290">[282]</a></sup>。所幸是海洋环境有着自我清洁的特性，清理海洋油污的细菌随着时间的推移自然出现，在墨西哥湾已经出现了以油污为食的细菌，这些细菌只花了几天的时间就把该区域泄漏的油污清理完<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-291"><a href="#cite_note-291">[283]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.B5.B7.E4.B8.8A.E6.B0.91.E6.97.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="海上民族">海上民族</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：海上民族">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一些在<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E6%B4%8B%E4%B8%9C%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%9A" title="海洋东南亚">海洋东南亚</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%81%8A%E7%89%A7%E6%B0%91%E6%97%8F" title="游牧民族">游牧民族</a>土着族群居住在船艇上，并从海里获得几乎所需要的全部东西。<a href="/wiki/%E8%8E%AB%E8%82%AF%E4%BA%BA" title="莫肯人">莫肯人</a>位在<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%9B%BD" title="泰国">泰国</a>的海岸、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%AC%E7%94%B8" title="缅甸">缅甸</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%89%E8%BE%BE%E6%9B%BC%E6%B5%B7" title="安达曼海">安达曼海</a>的岛屿<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-292"><a href="#cite_note-292">[284]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E7%91%B6%E6%97%8F" title="巴瑶族">巴瑶族</a>源自<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%8F%E7%A6%84%E7%BE%A4%E5%B2%9B" title="苏禄群岛">苏禄群岛</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%A3%89%E5%85%B0%E8%80%81%E5%B2%9B" title="棉兰老岛">棉兰老岛</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E5%A9%86%E7%BD%97%E6%B4%B2" title="婆罗洲">婆罗洲</a>北面<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-293"><a href="#cite_note-293">[285]</a></sup>。一些<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%89%E6%99%AE%E8%B3%BD%E4%BA%BA" title="吉普赛人">吉普赛人</a>精于<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E6%BD%9B%E6%B0%B4" title="自由潜水">自由潜水</a>，能够下潜到30米（98英尺）水深，然而他们习惯于较安定的陆上生活<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-294"><a href="#cite_note-294">[286]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-295"><a href="#cite_note-295">[287]</a></sup>。
</p><p>北极的土着人民，例如<a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%9A%E7%A7%91%E5%A5%87%E4%BA%BA" title="楚科奇人">楚科奇人</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E7%BA%BD%E7%89%B9%E4%BA%BA" title="因纽特人">因纽特人</a>、Inuit 原住民族及<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%A4%E7%9A%AE%E5%85%8B%E4%BA%BA" title="尤皮克人">尤皮克人</a>会捕擸海洋哺乳动物，包括<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E8%B1%B9" title="海豹">海豹</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%B2%B8%E9%B1%BC" title="鲸鱼">鲸鱼</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-296"><a href="#cite_note-296">[288]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E6%89%98%E9%9B%B7%E6%96%AF%E6%B5%B7%E5%B3%A1%E5%B2%9B%E6%B0%91" title="托雷斯海峡岛民">托雷斯海峡岛民</a>声称拥有<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E5%A0%A1%E7%A4%81" title="大堡礁">大堡礁</a>的所有权，他们在岛屿上以传统方式生活，包括狩猎，钓鱼，种植和与在附近的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E5%B8%83%E4%BA%9A%E6%96%B0%E5%87%A0%E5%86%85%E4%BA%9A" title="巴布亚新几内亚">巴布亚新几内亚</a>人和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BE%B3%E6%B4%B2" title="澳洲">澳洲</a>人交易<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-297"><a href="#cite_note-297">[289]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.88.87.E5.A4.A7.E6.B5.B7.E6.9C.89.E9.97.9C.E7.9A.84.E6.96.87.E5.8C.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="与大海有关的文化">与大海有关的文化</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：与大海有关的文化">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%96%87%E5%8C%96%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E6%B5%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="文化中的海（页面不存在）">文化中的海</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AssyrianWarship.jpg"><img alt="WA 124772: An Assyrian warship carved into stone (700–692 BC) from the reign of Sennacherib. Ninevah, South-West Palace, Room VII, Panel 11. British Museum." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="874" data-file-width="1197" decoding="async" height="161" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/AssyrianWarship.jpg/220px-AssyrianWarship.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/AssyrianWarship.jpg/330px-AssyrianWarship.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/AssyrianWarship.jpg/440px-AssyrianWarship.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AssyrianWarship.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>An <a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%9A%E8%BF%B0" title="亚述">Assyrian</a> relief from c. 700 BC showing <a href="#Animals">fish and a crab</a> swimming around a <a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%99%E5%B1%A4%E6%A7%B3%E5%BA%A7%E6%88%B0%E8%88%B9" title="双层桨座战船">双层桨座战船</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>在大众文化中，海的角色是十分矛盾的：既强大又安祥，美丽而又危险<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stow_8-18"><a href="#cite_note-Stow-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">（p. 10）</sup>。在神话、宗教、文学、艺术、诗歌、电影、戏剧和音乐中，其都扮演了一定的角色<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Westerdahl_298-0"><a href="#cite_note-Westerdahl-298">[290]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E4%BB%A3%E5%8F%B2" title="古代史">古人</a>相信，大海是受到<a href="/wiki/%E6%B0%B4%E7%A5%9E" title="水神">水神</a>所控制的，故在发生各种与海有关的灾难时，需用各种方法使水神的负面情绪平息。不同文化的水神各有不同，例如《<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%96%E7%B6%93" title="圣经">圣经</a>》中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%A9%E7%BB%B4%E5%9D%A6" title="利维坦">利维坦</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-299"><a href="#cite_note-299">[291]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A%E7%A5%9E%E8%AF%9D" title="希腊神话">希腊神话</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E5%BA%93%E6%8B%89" title="斯库拉">斯库拉</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-300"><a href="#cite_note-300">[292]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC%E7%A5%9E%E8%A9%B1" title="日本神话">日本神话</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%A3%AF%E9%BE%8D%E6%8D%B2" title="矶龙卷">矶龙卷</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-301"><a href="#cite_note-301">[293]</a></sup>、以及<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%97%E6%AC%A7%E7%A5%9E%E8%AF%9D" title="北欧神话">北欧神话</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%AA%E5%A8%81%E6%B5%B7%E6%80%AA" title="挪威海怪">挪威海怪</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-302"><a href="#cite_note-302">[294]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cotterell_303-0"><a href="#cite_note-Cotterell-303">[295]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">（pp. 206–208）</sup>。大海亦常见出现于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Christian imagery" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基督教意像"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99%E6%84%8F%E5%83%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基督教意像（页面不存在）">基督教意像</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christian_imagery" title="en:Christian imagery"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Christian imagery</span></a></span>）</span></span>中，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%80%B6%E7%A9%8C" title="耶稣">耶稣</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%BF%E5%BE%92_(%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99)" title="使徒 (基督教)">使徒</a>当中，就有几个原在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%A0%E5%88%A9%E5%88%A9%E6%B5%B7" title="加利利海">加利利海</a>工作的渔民。
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg"><img alt='"The Great Wave off Kanagawa" by Katsushika Hokusai. c. 1830.' class="thumbimage" data-file-height="5640" data-file-width="8242" decoding="async" height="151" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg/220px-Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg/330px-Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg/440px-Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Great_Wave_off_Kanagawa2.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E8%91%9B%E9%A5%B0%E5%8C%97%E6%96%8B" title="葛饰北斋">葛饰北斋</a>于1829年开始绘画的《<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E5%A5%88%E5%B7%9D%E6%B2%96%E6%B5%AA%E8%A3%8F" title="神奈川冲浪裏">神奈川冲浪裏</a>》，它是《<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%A8%E5%B6%BD%E4%B8%89%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%99%AF" title="冨岳三十六景">冨岳三十六景</a>》的首景。</div></div></div>
<p>在艺术此一领域中，人们对大海及与海有关的船只和生物的描绘多不胜数，从简单的像法国<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8E%B1%E5%A1%9E%E9%BD%90%E8%80%B6%E5%BE%B7%E6%B3%B0%E9%98%BF%E5%85%8B-%E8%A5%BF%E5%8B%92%E4%BC%8A&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="莱塞齐耶德泰阿克-西勒伊（页面不存在）">莱塞齐耶德泰阿克-西勒伊</a>的洞穴壁画或早期<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99%E8%97%9D%E8%A1%93" title="基督教艺术">基督教艺术</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E8%80%B6%E7%A9%8C%E9%AD%9A" title="耶稣鱼">耶稣鱼</a>，以至稍微复杂一点的则有<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%B7%E8%98%AD%E9%BB%83%E9%87%91%E6%99%82%E4%BB%A3%E7%B9%AA%E7%95%AB" title="荷兰黄金时代绘画">荷兰画家</a><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hendrik Cornelisz Vroom" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="亨德里克·弗鲁姆"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%A8%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E5%BC%97%E9%B2%81%E5%A7%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="亨德里克·弗鲁姆（页面不存在）">亨德里克·弗鲁姆</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hendrik_Cornelisz_Vroom" title="en:Hendrik Cornelisz Vroom"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hendrik Cornelisz Vroom</span></a></span>）</span></span>的作品，甚至复杂得像<a href="/wiki/%E8%91%9B%E9%A5%B0%E5%8C%97%E6%96%8B" title="葛饰北斋">葛饰北斋</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%AE%E4%B8%96%E7%B9%AA" title="浮世绘">浮世绘</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%A9%E6%96%AF%E6%B4%9B%C2%B7%E9%9C%8D%E9%BB%98" title="温斯洛·霍默">温斯洛·霍默</a>所绘画的海景。荷兰黄金时期的画家如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jan Porcellis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="扬·波赛利斯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%89%AC%C2%B7%E6%B3%A2%E8%B5%9B%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="扬·波赛利斯（页面不存在）">扬·波赛利斯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jan_Porcellis" title="en:Jan Porcellis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jan Porcellis</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hendrick Dubbels" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="亨德里克·杜博思"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%A8%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E6%9D%9C%E5%8D%9A%E6%80%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="亨德里克·杜博思（页面不存在）">亨德里克·杜博思</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hendrick_Dubbels" title="en:Hendrick Dubbels"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hendrick Dubbels</span></a></span>）</span></span>、威廉·范德维德<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Willem van de Velde the Elder" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="老威廉·范德维德"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%80%81%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E8%8C%83%E5%BE%B7%E7%BB%B4%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="老威廉·范德维德（页面不存在）">父</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willem_van_de_Velde_the_Elder" title="en:Willem van de Velde the Elder"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Willem van de Velde the Elder</span></a></span>）</span></span>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Willem van de Velde the Elder" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="小威廉·范德维德"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%8F%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E8%8C%83%E5%BE%B7%E7%BB%B4%E5%BE%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="小威廉·范德维德（页面不存在）">子</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willem_van_de_Velde_the_Elder" title="en:Willem van de Velde the Elder"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Willem van de Velde the Elder</span></a></span>）</span></span>和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ludolf Bakhuizen" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="卢多尔夫·巴克赫伊森"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%A2%E5%A4%9A%E5%B0%94%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E5%85%8B%E8%B5%AB%E4%BC%8A%E6%A3%AE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="卢多尔夫·巴克赫伊森（页面不存在）">卢多尔夫·巴克赫伊森</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ludolf_Bakhuizen" title="en:Ludolf Bakhuizen"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ludolf Bakhuizen</span></a></span>）</span></span>都曾在他们的作品中赞美过海洋以及军力巅峰时的<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%B7%E8%98%AD%E7%9A%87%E5%AE%B6%E6%B5%B7%E8%BB%8D" title="荷兰皇家海军">荷兰皇家海军</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Slive_304-0"><a href="#cite_note-Slive-304">[296]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-305"><a href="#cite_note-305">[297]</a></sup>
</p><p>音乐也从海洋中获得了许多灵感。平静的水面、汹涌的波浪和海上的风暴，这些意象都被水手们吟唱在<a href="/wiki/%E8%88%B9%E5%A4%AB%E5%8F%B7%E5%AD%90" title="船夫号子">船夫号子</a>中，来帮助他们在艰难的任务中协调步调。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-306"><a href="#cite_note-306">[298]</a></sup>与海相关的古典音乐有<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%86%E6%9F%A5%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E7%93%A6%E6%A0%BC%E7%BA%B3" title="理查德·瓦格纳">理查德·瓦格纳</a>的《<a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%82%E6%B3%8A%E7%9A%84%E8%8D%B7%E8%98%AD%E4%BA%BA_(%E6%AD%8C%E5%8A%87)" title="漂泊的荷兰人 (歌剧)">漂泊的荷兰人</a>》<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-307"><a href="#cite_note-307">[299]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94-%E5%85%8B%E6%B4%9B%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E5%BE%B7%E5%BD%AA%E8%A5%BF" title="阿希尔-克洛德·德彪西">克洛德·德彪西</a>的《<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E6%B5%B7_(%E5%BE%B7%E5%B8%83%E8%A5%BF)" title="大海 (德布西)">海</a>》（1903-1905年）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-308"><a href="#cite_note-308">[300]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%A5%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E7%BB%B4%E5%88%A9%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6%E7%A6%8F" title="查尔斯·维利尔斯·斯坦福">查尔斯·维利尔斯·斯坦福</a>的《海洋之歌》（1904年）和《舰队之歌》（1910年）、<a href="/wiki/%E7%88%B1%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%8E%C2%B7%E5%9F%83%E5%B0%94%E5%8A%A0" title="爱德华·埃尔加">爱德华·埃尔加</a>的《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sea Pictures" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="海景"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7%E6%99%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="海景（页面不存在）">海景</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sea_Pictures" title="en:Sea Pictures"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sea Pictures</span></a></span>）</span></span>》（1899年）及<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B7%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E4%BD%9B%E6%BC%A2%C2%B7%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%E6%96%AF" title="雷夫·佛汉·威廉斯">雷夫·佛汉·威廉斯</a>的《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="A Sea Symphony" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="海之交响曲"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7%E4%B9%8B%E4%BA%A4%E9%9F%BF%E6%9B%B2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="海之交响曲（页面不存在）">海之交响曲</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Sea_Symphony" title="en:A Sea Symphony"><span dir="auto" lang="en">A Sea Symphony</span></a></span>）</span></span>》（1903-1909年）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-309"><a href="#cite_note-309">[301]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg"><img alt="Winslow Homer, The Gulf Stream (1899). Oil on canvas; 71.5 x 124.8 cm. Metropolitan Museum of Art." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3540" data-file-width="5886" decoding="async" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg/220px-Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg/330px-Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg/440px-Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Winslow_Homer_-_The_Gulf_Stream_-_Metropolitan_Museum_of_Art.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><i><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="The Gulf Stream (painting)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="The Gulf Stream (painting)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Gulf_Stream_(painting)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Gulf Stream (painting)（页面不存在）">The Gulf Stream</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Gulf_Stream_(painting)" title="en:The Gulf Stream (painting)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">The Gulf Stream (painting)</span></a></span>）</span></span></i> (1899) by <a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%A9%E6%96%AF%E6%B4%9B%C2%B7%E9%9C%8D%E9%BB%98" title="温斯洛·霍默">Winslow Homer</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>海，作为一个象征，几个世纪以来一直在文学和诗歌中反复出现。有时，它只是一个切入背景，而且总会引入像风暴、海难、战斗、苦难、灾难、希望的曙光亦或是死亡<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-310"><a href="#cite_note-310">[302]</a></sup>。在写于公元前8世纪的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%B2%E8%AF%97" title="史诗">史诗</a>《<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%A5%E5%BE%B7%E8%B5%9B" title="奥德赛">奥德赛</a>》中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Odyssey_311-0"><a href="#cite_note-Odyssey-311">[303]</a></sup>，<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%B7%E9%A9%AC" title="荷马">荷马</a>描述了希腊英雄<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%A5%E5%BE%B7%E4%BF%AE%E6%96%AF" title="奥德修斯">奥德修斯</a>在《<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9A%E7%89%B9" title="伊利亚特">伊利亚特</a>》中的战争结束后十年艰苦的返乡航程中所经历的诸多劫难<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-312"><a href="#cite_note-312">[304]</a></sup>。在日本诗人<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%BE%E5%B0%BE%E8%8A%AD%E8%95%89" title="松尾芭蕉">松尾芭蕉</a>（1644–1694）的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%B3%E5%8F%A5" title="俳句">俳句</a>诗歌中，海也是一个反复出现的主题<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-313"><a href="#cite_note-313">[305]</a></sup>。在现代文学中，像<a href="/wiki/%E8%B5%AB%E5%B0%94%E6%9B%BC%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E5%B0%94%E7%BB%B4%E5%B0%94" title="赫尔曼·梅尔维尔">赫尔曼·梅尔维尔</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-314"><a href="#cite_note-314">[306]</a></sup>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joseph Conrad's career at sea" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="约瑟夫·康拉德的海上生涯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B4%84%E7%91%9F%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E5%BA%B7%E6%8B%89%E5%BE%B7%E7%9A%84%E6%B5%B7%E4%B8%8A%E7%94%9F%E6%B6%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="约瑟夫·康拉德的海上生涯（页面不存在）">约瑟夫·康拉德</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Conrad%27s_career_at_sea" title="en:Joseph Conrad's career at sea"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joseph Conrad's career at sea</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-315"><a href="#cite_note-315">[307]</a></sup>及<a href="/wiki/%E8%B5%AB%E5%B0%94%E6%9B%BC%C2%B7%E6%B2%83%E5%85%8B" title="赫尔曼·沃克">赫尔曼·沃克</a>这样的海员也创作过许多受海启发的小说<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-316"><a href="#cite_note-316">[308]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%BE%E7%A5%9E%E7%97%85%E5%AD%A6" title="精神病学">精神病学</a>家<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E8%8D%A3%E6%A0%BC" title="卡尔·荣格">卡尔·荣格</a>认为，在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8A%E6%A2%A6" title="释梦">释梦</a>的时候，海象征着<a href="/wiki/%E6%BD%9B%E6%84%8F%E8%AD%98" title="潜意识">个人</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E4%BD%93%E6%BD%9C%E6%84%8F%E8%AF%86" title="集体潜意识">集体无意识</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jung_317-0"><a href="#cite_note-Jung-317">[309]</a></sup>。尽管地球上生命的起源仍然是个争论中的问题<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-318"><a href="#cite_note-318">[310]</a></sup>，自然学家<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B7%E5%88%87%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E5%8D%A1%E6%A3%AE" title="雷切尔·卡森">雷切尔·卡森</a>却还是在《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="The Sea Around Us" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="我们周围的海洋"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%88%91%E5%80%91%E5%91%A8%E5%9C%8D%E7%9A%84%E6%B5%B7%E6%B4%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="我们周围的海洋（页面不存在）">我们周围的海洋</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Sea_Around_Us" title="en:The Sea Around Us"><span dir="auto" lang="en">The Sea Around Us</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中写道：“生命的源头是海洋，它孕育了种种生物，现在却被其中一种生物的活动所威胁，这是多么奇怪的情形啊。不过，虽然海洋环境不断恶化，但是这片无边的大洋仍然会继续存在下去，实际上，生物本身才是真正的受害者。”<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-winchester_319-0"><a href="#cite_note-winchester-319">[311]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E9.87.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="notelist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">一种定义视海为海洋的分支，尽管现在<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%8B%E9%9A%9B%E6%B5%B7%E9%81%93%E6%B8%AC%E9%87%8F%E7%B5%84%E7%B9%94" title="国际海道测量组织">国际海道测量组织</a>以一种被视为合乎习俗但相当主观的方式<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> 将世界上海洋的边界按照没有被另外包括于海中的海域来定义<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ihorg_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-ihorg-7">[7]</a></sup>。另一种说法认为“海”是对于一个大部分被陆地包围的水体的简称<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>，这种说法就没有包括<a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%B0%BE%E8%97%BB%E6%B5%B7" title="马尾藻海">马尾藻海</a>的情况。第三种理论认为海以<a href="#Basin">海盆</a>为底，这种说法包含了<a href="/wiki/%E8%A3%8F%E6%B5%B7" title="裏海">里海</a>的情形，因为里海曾经是古代一片海洋的一部分。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-17">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">相应地，这一公约并不适用于<a href="/wiki/%E8%A3%8F%E6%B5%B7" title="裏海">里海</a>的情况，在<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%B3%95" title="国际法">法律</a>角度中它被视为“国际湖泊”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[15]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-25"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-25">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Hydrous <a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%96%E6%99%B6%E6%A9%84%E6%A6%84%E7%9F%B3" title="尖晶橄榄石">ringwoodite</a> recovered from <a href="/wiki/%E7%81%AB%E5%B1%B1%E5%99%B4%E7%99%BC%E9%A1%9E%E5%9E%8B" title="火山喷发类型">volcanic eruptions</a> suggests that the mantle transition zone between the <a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E5%B9%94" title="地幔">lower</a> and <a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E5%B9%94" title="地幔">upper mantle</a> holds between one<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[19]</a></sup> and three<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[20]</a></sup> times as much water as all of the world's surface oceans combined. Experiments to recreate the conditions of the lower mantle suggest it may contain still more water as well, as much as five times the mass of water present in the world's oceans.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[21]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[22]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-36"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-36">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%BA" title="人">Human</a> <a href="/wiki/%E8%85%8E" title="肾">kidney</a>s excrete <a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BF" title="尿">urine</a> that is around 2% saline,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10hut_34-0"><a href="#cite_note-10hut-34">[31]</a></sup> so that drinking one liter of most forms of seawater will require drinking at least another liter of freshwater to prevent <span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sodium in biology#Human water and salt balance" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Sodium in biology#Human water and salt balance"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Sodium_in_biology&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sodium in biology（页面不存在）">harmful</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sodium_in_biology#Human_water_and_salt_balance" title="en:Sodium in biology"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sodium in biology#Human water and salt balance</span></a></span>）</span></span> excesses of sodium. Without this additional water, increased urination to remove the salt produces <a href="/wiki/%E8%84%B1%E6%B0%B4" title="脱水">dehydration</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[32]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-103"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-103">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"> To help put a change of this magnitude into perspective, when the pH of human blood plasma is raised from its normal 7.4 to a value above 7.8, or lowered to a value below 6.8, death ensues.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tanner2012_102-0"><a href="#cite_note-Tanner2012-102">[98]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-134"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-134">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Given that the most likely landfall regions have been under 50米（160英尺） of water since the end of the <a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%AB%E6%AC%A1%E5%86%B0%E6%9C%9F" title="末次冰期">last ice age</a>, it is unlikely that the timing will ever be established with certainty.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-scocane_131-0"><a href="#cite_note-scocane-131">[126]</a></sup> Two common theories are a crossing from <a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%9D%E6%B1%B6" title="帝汶">Timor</a> to the northwest Australian mainland around 70,000 years ago and a crossing from <a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%8F%E6%8B%89%E5%A8%81%E8%A5%BF%E5%B2%9B" title="苏拉威西岛">Sulawesi</a> to <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%B9%BE%E5%85%A7%E4%BA%9E" title="新几内亚">New Guinea</a> around 50,000 years ago,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-scocane_131-1"><a href="#cite_note-scocane-131">[126]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132">[127]</a></sup> possibly assisted by a <a href="#Tsunami">tsunami</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[128]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-147"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-147">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E9%BD%90%E5%BA%93%E6%96%AF" title="基齐库斯">Greek</a> navigator <a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E9%BD%90%E5%BA%93%E6%96%AF%E7%9A%84%E6%AC%A7%E5%A4%9A%E5%85%8B%E7%B4%A2%E6%96%AF" title="基齐库斯的欧多克索斯">Eudoxus</a> was later <span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Geography (Strabo)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Geography (Strabo)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Geography_(Strabo)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Geography (Strabo)（页面不存在）">reported</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geography_(Strabo)" title="en:Geography (Strabo)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Geography (Strabo)</span></a></span>）</span></span> by <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%B3%A2" title="斯特拉波">Strabo</a> to have accidentally discovered a wrecked ship from <a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%A0%E7%9A%84%E6%96%AF" title="加的斯">Gades</a> on the north<i>east</i> coast of Africa and to have then attempted two (failed) circumnavigations of Africa around 116 BC.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[140]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-194"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-194">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E6%B0%B4" title="内水">内水</a>渔获量以固定的幅度成长，由1950年代的每年300万公吨到2010年的每年1100万公吨，但仍不到总渔获量的10%<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-olderfishstats_193-1"><a href="#cite_note-olderfishstats-193">[186]</a></sup></span>
</li>
</ol>
</div>

<li id="cite_note-188"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-188">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><span lang="grc">Ἰσίδωρος Χαρακηνός</span> Isidore of Charax). <span lang="grc">Τὸ τῆς Παρθίας Περιηγητικόν</span> [<i>Tò tēs Parthías Periēgētikón</i>, <i>A Journey around Parthia</i>]. c. 1st century AD <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#54595d; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到古希腊语网页">（古希腊文）</span> in <span lang="grc">Ἀθήναιος</span> (<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E7%89%B9%E7%B4%8D%E5%A5%A7%E6%96%AF" title="阿特纳奥斯">Athenaeus</a>). <span lang="grc">Δειπνοσοφισταί</span> [<i>Deipnosophistaí</i>, <i><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Deipnosophistae" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Deipnosophistae"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Deipnosophistae&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Deipnosophistae（页面不存在）">The Dinner Experts</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deipnosophistae" title="en:Deipnosophistae"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Deipnosophistae</span></a></span>）</span></span></i>], Book III, 93E. c. 3rd century <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#54595d; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到古希腊语网页">（古希腊文）</span> Trans. <h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.80.A3.E7.B5.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部连结">外部连结</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B5%B7&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：外部连结">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
